paymentDateAdjustment) {\n142: \n143:     ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n144:     ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n145: \n146:     // for a vanilla call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n147:     // for a vanilla put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n148:     double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n149:     double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n150:     double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n151:     CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getBase(), baseAmount);\n152:     CurrencyAmount counterCurrencyAmount = ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n\n    // for a European call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n    // for a European put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n    double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n    double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n    double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n    CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, Full system test\n\n### Parallelization Opportunities\n- Core class renames can happen in parallel after dependencies are clear\n- Test file renames can happen independently after core renames\n- Test import updates can happen in parallel\n\n---\n\n## Validation Checklist\n\nBefore considering this refactoring complete:\n\n- [ ] All 13 core files renamed (check solution.md FILE_CHANGES_SUMMARY.md)\n- [ ] All 14 test files renamed (check FILE_CHANGES_SUMMARY.md)\n- [ ] All 23 supporting files updated (check FILE_CHANGES_SUMMARY.md)\n- [ ] No `FxVanillaOption` references remain (except in comments/strings)\n- [ ] No `FxVanillaOptionTrade` references remain (except in comments/strings)\n- [ ] No `ResolvedFxVanillaOption` references remain (except in comments/strings)\n- [ ] `ProductType.FX_EUROPEAN_OPTION` exists (not `FX_VANILLA_OPTION`)\n- [ ] `writeFxEuropeanOption()` method exists (not `writeFxVanillaOption()`)\n- [ ] All product, pricer, measure, and loader modules compile\n- [ ] Full test suite passes\n- [ ] No compilation warnings related to undefined types\n\n---\n\n## Related Files\n\n### Renamed Example (provided)\n- `/workspace/FxEuropeanOption.java` - Shows how the renamed core class should look\n\n### Documentation\n- `solution.md` - Complete technical analysis\n- `IMPLEMENTATION_GUIDE.md` - Line-by-line implementation steps\n- `FILE_CHANGES_SUMMARY.md` - File inventory and implementation order\n\n---\n\n## Questions?\n\nRefer to the specific documentation file:\n- **\"What files are affected?\"** → FILE_CHANGES_SUMMARY.md\n- **\"How do I implement changes to Product class?\"** → IMPLEMENTATION_GUIDE.md Phase 1\n- **\"How do I implement changes to Pricer class?\"** → IMPLEMENTATION_GUIDE.md Phase 2\n- **\"What's the dependency chain?\"** → solution.md \"Dependency Chain\"\n- **\"What should I verify?\"** → solution.md \"Verification Checklist\"\n\n---\n\n## Version Control\n\nRecommended git approach:\n1. Refactoring Strategy\n\nThis refactoring follows a **dependency-driven approach** to ensure compilation success at each step:\n\n1. **Rename Core Classes First** - The 4 core Joda-Beans classes (`FxVanillaOption`, `FxVanillaOptionTrade`, `ResolvedFxVanillaOption`, `ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade`) form the foundation. Everything else depends on them.\n\n2. **Rename Pricer Classes** - The 4 pricer classes depend directly on core classes. They're renamed second to maintain dependency order.\n\n3. **Update Barrier Option Classes** - `FxSingleBarrierOption` and `ResolvedFxSingleBarrierOption` wrap the core classes, so field types are updated.\n\n4. **Rename Measure Classes** - The 4 measure classes depend on the renamed pricers, so they're renamed third.\n\n5. **Update Constants & Utilities** - `ProductType.FX_VANILLA_OPTION` constant and CSV utility methods are updated.\n\n6. **Rename Tests Last** - All test files are renamed to match their classes and all imports updated.\n\n### Why This Order Matters\n\n```\nPhase 1: Core Classes (4 files)\n  ↓\nPhase 2: Pricers (4 files) - depend on core\n  ↓\nPhase 3: Measure Classes (4 files) - depend on pricers\n  ↓\nPhase 4: Update dependent files (20+ files) - import the above\n  ↓\nPhase 5: Tests (25+ files) - import everything\n```\n\nIf you attempt to rename measure classes before pricers, the imports will fail. If you rename core classes without updating barrier options, compilation breaks. This dependency chain ensures each phase compiles successfully.\n\n### Areas Impacted\n\n- **Product Module** - Core product classes and wrappers\n- **Pricer Module** - Black/Vanna-Volga pricers and barrier pricers\n- **Measure Module** - Calculations, functions, and method enums\n- **Loader Module** - CSV plugin and utilities\n- **Tests** - 50+ test files across all modules\n\n### Backward Compatibility\n\nThis is a **breaking change**:\n- Public type names change\n- Method signatures change\n- Constants are renamed\n- CSV type strings change (affects persisted data)\n\nThis requires a major version bump and migration guide for users upgrading.\n\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":7,"cache_creation_input_tokens":792,"cache_read_input_tokens":117843,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":792},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"697db78f-cfc5-49e5-9898-8bb1e5a5fdd9","uuid":"2cad8705-3f03-4132-a85e-e0747a5f6c21"}
